class=\"terms\">PATIENT AGREEMENT AND CONSENT</h1><p><b>BY CLICKING AGREE, YOU ACKNOWLEDGE THAT YOU HAVE READ, ACCEPTED, AND AGREED TO BE BOUND BY THIS PATIENT AGREEMENT AND CONSENT.  IF YOU DO NOT AGREE TO THIS PATIENT AGREEMENT AND CONSENT, CLICK ON THE DISAGREE BUTTON. YOU HEREBY GRANT AGENCY AUTHORITY TO ANY PARTY WHO CLICKS ON THE AGREE BUTTON ON YOUR BEHALF.</b></p><p><!-- react-text: 108 -->In this Patient Agreement and Consent (this <!-- /react-text --><b>Agreement</b><!-- react-text: 110 -->), the terms you and yours refer to the person who is creating a patient account with Forward, or in the case of a minor, you and yours refer to and include (i) the parent or legal guardian who provides consent to the creation of such account by such minor, and (ii) the minor for whom consent is being provided. <!-- /react-text --></p><ol><li><!-- react-text: 113 -->Forward. <!-- /react-text --><p>Forward (Forward, we or us) is a California professional corporation that employs and/or contracts with physicians and allied health professionals to provide medical services to individuals residing in California.  Forward is a new kind of doctors office that reimagines the experience from the patient perspective and incorporates modern technology.  Forward works closely with GoForward Inc. (GoForward), a technology company that provides technological and administrative support for Forward and owns and operates the GoForward website located at https://goforward.com and the GoForward mobile application (collectively, the Platform), anything associated therewith, including its content (Content) and any products or services provided through the Platform or otherwise by GoForward (collectively, including the Platform and the Content, the Service).  </p></li><li><!-- react-text: 116 -->Consent to Use of Technology and Telehealth in the Delivery of Care.<!-- /react-text --><p>As a patient of Forward, you may be consulting with Forward healthcare providers, including physicians, nurses and other health professionals (Providers) via the use of telehealth, whether through the Service or otherwise, and/or your Providers may use or rely upon certain technology in the delivery of your care.  Telehealth involves the delivery of healthcare services using electronic communications, information technology or other means between a healthcare provider and a patient who are not in the same physical location. Telehealth may be used for diagnosis, treatment, follow-up and/or patient education, and may include, but is not limited to, one or more of the following:</p><ul><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Electronic transmission of medical records, photo images, personal health information or other data between a patient and a healthcare provider</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Interactions between a patient and healthcare provider via audio, video and/or data communications</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Use of output data from medical devices, sound and video files</li></ul><p>The electronic systems used in the Service will incorporate network and software security protocols to protect the privacy and security of your information, and will include measures to safeguard data against intentional or unintentional corruption.</p><p><b>Anticipated Benefits:  </b></p><p>The use of telehealth and other technology by your Provider(s) may have the following possible benefits:</p><ul><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Making it easier and more efficient for you to access medical care and treatment for the conditions treated by such Provider(s) </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Allowing you to obtain medical care and treatment by Provider(s) at times that are convenient for you</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Enabling you to interact with Provider(s) without the necessity of an in-office appointment</li></ul><p><b>Possible Risks:</b></p><p>While the use of telehealth and other technology in the delivery of care can provide potential benefits for you, there are also potential risks associated with the use of telehealth and other technology. These risks include, but may not be limited to the following:</p><ul><li class=\"static-docs-li\">The quality, accuracy or effectiveness of the services you receive from your Provider could be limited.  </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Technology, including the Service, may contain bugs or other errors, including ones which may limit functionality, produce erroneous results, render part or all of such technology, including the Service, unavailable or inoperable, produce incorrect records, transmissions, data or content, or cause records, transmissions, data or content to be corrupted or lost.  Failures of technology may also impact your Provider(s) ability to correctly diagnose or treat your medical condition.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">The inability of your Provider(s) to conduct certain tests or assess vital signs in-person may in some cases prevent the Provider(s) from providing a diagnosis or treatment or from identifying the need for emergency medical care or treatment for you.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Your Provider(s) may not able to provide medical treatment for your particular condition and you may be required to seek alternative healthcare or emergency care services.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Delays in medical evaluation/treatment could occur due to unavailability of your Provider(s) or deficiencies or failures of the technology or electronic equipment used. </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">The electronic systems or other security protocols or safeguards used could fail, causing a breach of privacy of your medical or other information.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Given regulatory requirements in certain jurisdictions, your Provider(s) diagnosis and/or treatment options, especially pertaining to certain prescriptions, may be limited.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">A lack of access to all of your medical records may result in adverse drug interactions or allergic reactions or other judgment errors.</li></ul><p><b>By clicking AGREE you understand, agree and provide your consent, on behalf of yourself and the minor child for whom you are establishing an account, with respect to the following:</b></p><ul><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Certain technology, including the Service, may be used by us or your Providers while still in a beta testing and development phase, and before such technology is a final and finished product.  </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">Technology we use to deliver care, including the Service, may contain bugs or other errors, including ones which may limit functionality, produce erroneous results, render part or all of such technology unavailable or inoperable, produce incorrect records, transmissions, data or content, or cause records, transmissions, data or content to be corrupted or lost, any or all of which could limit or otherwise impact the quality, accuracy and/or effectiveness of the medical care or other services that you receive from your Provider(s).</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">The delivery of healthcare services via telehealth is an evolving field and the use of telehealth or other technology in your medical care and treatment from Provider(s) may include uses of technology different from those described in this Agreement or not specifically described in this Agreement.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">No potential benefits from the use of telehealth or other technology or specific results can be guaranteed. Your condition may not be cured or improved, and in some cases, may get worse.  </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">There are limitations in the provision of medical care and treatment via telehealth and technology, including the Service, and you may not be able to receive diagnosis and/or treatment through telehealth for every condition for which you seek diagnosis and/or treatment. </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">There are potential risks to the use of telehealth and other technology, including but not limited to the risks described in this Agreement.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You have the opportunity to discuss the use of telehealth and technology, including the Service, with your Provider(s), including the benefits and risks of such use and the alternatives to the use of telehealth.  </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You have the right to withdraw your consent to the use of telehealth and technology in the course of your care set forth in this Section 2 at any time, which you may exercise by providing written notice to Forward at 660 4th St. #202, San Francisco, CA 94107 and to GoForward at 660 4th St. #202, San Francisco, CA 94107. Due to the degree of integration of technology in Forwards delivery of care, the withdrawal of such consent may prevent you from obtaining some or all of the services Forward offers. Any withdrawal of your consent will be effective upon receipt of the written notice described above, except that such withdrawal will not have any effect on any action taken by GoForward, Forward or your Provider(s) in reliance on this Agreement before it received your written notice of withdrawal.  Any withdrawal of your consent will not affect any other provision of this Agreement, and you will continue to be bound by this Agreement.  </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You understand that the use of telehealth involves electronic communication of your personal medical information to Provider(s).    </li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You understand that it is your duty to provide GoForward, Forward and your Provider(s) truthful, accurate and complete information, including all relevant information regarding care that you may have received or may be receiving from healthcare providers other than Forward.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You understand that each of your Provider(s) may determine in his or sole discretion that your condition is not suitable for diagnosis and/or treatment using telehealth technology, including the Service, and that you may need to seek medical care and treatment from your Provider(s), or a specialist or other healthcare provider, outside of such telehealth technology.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You acknowledge that some photographic or other images you submit to Forward, via the Service or otherwise, and that will be shared with Provider(s) may include portions of all of your breast or genitalia, and you hereby agree to the receipt of such images by your Provider(s) solely for the purposes of such Provider(s) providing you medical care and treatment.</li><li class=\"static-docs-li\">You represent that (a) you have read this Agreement carefully, (b) you understand the risks and benefits of the use of telehealth and other technology, including the Service, in the medical care and treatment provided to you by Provider(s), and (c) you have the legal capacity and authority to provide this consent for yourself and/or the minor for which you are consenting under applicable federal and state laws, including laws relating to the age of majority and/or parental/guardian consent.</li></ul></li><li><!-- react-text: 159 -->Medical Scribes.<!-- /react-text --><p><!-- react-text: 161 -->In order to ensure that the information you provide to your Provider(s) during your in-person appointments is effectively captured and included in our records, we have Forward employees who act as scribes for your conversations with your Provider(s).  These scribes are located outside of your treatment room and cannot see you, but they can hear your conversation with your Provider(s) and they input the information you tell your Provider(s) into our records. Your conversation is not recorded, but the scribes will be able to hear your conversation with your Provider(s). We believe that using these scribes allows your Provider(s) to focus on you while also ensuring your information is captured in your records. <!-- /react-text --><b>If you are not comfortable with the use of a scribe, you must inform Forward before your appointment with any Provider. Due to the integral role our scribes play in the way our practice and technology operate, if you do not agree to the use of a scribe, you will not be able to use Forwards services or meet with our Providers. By meeting with any Provider or failing to inform Forward of your objection to the use of a scribe, you are agreeing to the use of a scribe as described in this Agreement.</b></p></li><li><!-- react-text: 164 -->Genetic Testing.<!-- /react-text --><p>Forward works with a third-party genetic testing company to make available certain genetic testing for you. To participate in such genetic testing, you will be required to sign a separate Informed Consent for Genetic Testing (Genetic Testing Consent). If you sign a Genetic Testing Consent, the Genetic Testing Consent will be considered part of this Agreement and the terms and conditions of this Agreement, including the disclaimers, limitations of liability and binding arbitration/class waiver, will apply to any genetic testing performed for you.</p></li><li><!-- react-text: 167 -->Access to Medical Record Through Platform.<!-- /react-text --><p>To ensure that your medical records are readily accessible to you, Forward provides you with access  to certain components of your medical records through the Platform, including lab and genetic test results and other health data gathered by Forward and/or provided by you.  By clicking Agree and/or using the Service, you acknowledge and agree that your medical record will be accessible through the Platform, and that it is your responsibility to keep your computer, phone and other devices you use to access the Service secure.</p></li><li><!-- react-text: 170 -->Payment Terms.<!-- /react-text --><p>In order to become a patient of Forward, visit Providers and use the GoForward Service, you will need to purchase a subscription from Forward (a Subscription).  If you purchase a Subscription, we may ask you to supply additional information relevant to your purchase, including, without limitation, your credit card number, the expiration date of your credit card and your billing address (such information, Payment Information). You represent and warrant that you have the legal right to use all payment method(s) represented by any such Payment Information. When you initiate a purchase, you authorize us to provide your Payment Information to our third party payment processors so we can complete your purchase and charge your payment method(s) for the Subscription you have selected.  You may, in some cases, need to provide additional information to verify your identity before completing your purchase (such information is considered part of Payment Information by Forward and GoForward). You agree that your purchase of a Subscription is neither contingent on the delivery of any future services, functionality or features, nor dependent on any oral or written comments made by Forward, GoForward or the Providers regarding future services, functionality or features.</p><p>By agreeing to this Agreement and purchasing a Subscription, you acknowledge that your Subscription has recurring payment features and you accept responsibility for all recurring payment obligations prior to cancellation of your Subscription by you or Forward.
